474H 188V 10482X 14288C Mem:3 Exits:ESW> lThe Crossroads
Several roads meet at a large junction here. The road to the south
leads to the New Sea, while the roads west and east continue to delve
through the Plains. Far off to the west, a range of mountains can be seen.
There is a slight breeze thick with the spores from the plants and weed
that are so prevalent in the Plains.
A large sign has been hammered into the ground here.
A solemn knight of the sword patrols the area for draconians. (white aura)
Skogul Crowfriend, the Carnage of Ragnarok is standing here. (flying) (invisible) (red aura)
Nalle is standing here. (flying) (red aura)
. . . is enveloped in flames.
Manzanas the Menace is standing here. (flying) (invisible) (red aura)
